About Us
Pipefy is the workflow management software that increases team productivity and standardizes processes for teams like Finance, HR and Customer Service, so those requesting services, processing requests and managing the operation are more efficient. Through a low-code/no-code platform, Pipefy allows workers to independently automate manual tasks, move fast with ready-to-use, customizable workflows and deploy their own solutions. Digitally transform your processes in a matter of hours, not weeks or months.

Through innovation, we aspire to offer our customers the most attractive and efficient process management service.



About The Role
We are looking for people who are passionate about building robust and scalable systems to join our QA Team. Someone dynamic, self-directed, skillful and enthusiastic who takes ownership of their work and is committed to quality assurance.
Understand that our mission is to guarantee quality throughout the development process and direct efforts towards prevention and not only to find bugs.


What You'll Do
Use your analytical and technical skills to demonstrate success in devising and bringing a full test automation and also manually strategy to maturity and directly impact the quality of the software we create. You will work on a team focused on building product features from start to finish: concept, discovery, implementation, and maintenance.

Develop automated functional UI tests & API/Service level tests;
Improve the existing test automation tools to further increase their stability, maintainability, expandability, and usefulness to the team;
Will help improve processes that increase the quality of our products and work day;
Champion the efforts to achieve a high-quality standard;
Research and propose new solutions and technologies for our testing needs;
Outstanding communication in oral and written English;
Strong organizational skills.


What We Are Looking For
Technical knowledge:
Experience in Test Automation web frameworks such as Cypress, Selenium;
Experience with API test tools such as Postman or SoapUI;
Experience with programming languages (specially javascript and ruby);
Experience working with Cucumber, JBehave or other BDD frameworks;
Experience working with CI/CD tools;
Experience with Git;
Experience with Scrum and Kanban;

Soft Skills:
Problem-solving: identify the issue, analyze the causes, generate a set of alternatives, evaluate the best solutions, assess the effectiveness;
Business Oriented more than Technology Oriented - Your decisions and what you build impact our business. You go to what is needed for our business to achieve over choosing what is cool or in the hype of technology;
People First: You care about people! Your acts and what you build impact real people's lives;
Adaptive Learning;
Simple and straightforward solutions more than over-engineering;
Ability to work as part of a self-directed team, in which you determine your tasks on a daily basis in coordination with your team members.
